l-6.748-6.981L76.538,83.794z"/></g><g><path clip-rule="evenodd" d="M66.124,50.799c7.742,0,14.018,6.276,14.018,14.019 c0.091,0.304,0.158,0.559,0.215,0.801C76.31,63.901,76.404,64.735,76.404,65.586z M72.438,61.433 ## Instruction

Remove products of a specified model from your WooCommerce store and recall the corresponding products. The product must be taken off the shelf (set to draft or private status, or with catalog visibility set to hidden), rather than deleted. Given a product model, search for historical orders related to that product and send a recall email to the corresponding customer's email address. See `recall_email_template.md` for the email template. The email must include a Google Forms recall form created using the `recall_form_template.json` template, and return the form information in `recall_report.json`. The template is as follows:

```json
\{
"form_id": "Google Forms form ID",

"form_url": "Google Forms form link",
\}
```

<div className="tool-call-box">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  viewBox="0 0 48 48" width="14px" height="14px" style={{margin: 0, padding: 0, display: 'inline-block'}}><path fill="#FFA000" d="M40,12H22l-4-4H8c-2.2,0-4,1.8-4,4v8h40v-4C44,13.8,42.2,12,40,12z"/><path fill="#FFCA28" d="M40,12H8c-2.2,0-4,1.8-4,4v20c0,2.2,1.8,4,4,4h32c2.2,0,4-1.8,4-4V16C44,13.8,42.2,12,40,12z"/></svg> `filesystem-write_file`

```text workspace/product_recall_system.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Product Recall System for WooCommerce
This script handles the complete product recall process including:
1. Finding products by model
2. Setting products to draft/private status
3. Finding related orders
4. Creating recall forms
5. Sending recall emails to customers
"""

import json
import re
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional

class ProductRecallSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.recall_data = {
            "recalled_products": [],
            "affected_orders": [],
            "customers_notified": [],
            "form_info": {},
            "recall_date": datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
    
    def find_products_by_model(self, model_name: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """Find all products matching the specified model name"""
        print(f"Searching for products with model: {model_name}")
        
        # Search products by name/SKU/description
        products = []
        
        # Search by name
        try:
            name_results = self.woo_products_list(search=model_name)
            if name_results:
                products.extend(name_results)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error searching by name: {e}")
        
        # Search by SKU
        try:
            sku_results = self.woo_products_list(sku=model_name)
            if sku_results:
                products.extend(sku_results)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error searching by SKU: {e}")
        
        # Remove duplicates based on product ID
        unique_products = []
        seen_ids = set()
        for product in products:
            if product.get('id') not in seen_ids:
                unique_products.append(product)
                seen_ids.add(product.get('id'))
        
        print(f"Found {len(unique_products)} products matching model: {model_name}")
        return unique_products
    
    def recall_products(self, products: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """Set products to draft status (recall from market)"""
        recalled_products = []
        
        for product in products:
            try:
                product_id = product['id']
                print(f"Recalling product ID: {product_id} - {product.get('name', 'Unknown')}")
                
                # Update product to draft status and hidden visibility
                update_data = {
                    "status": "draft",
                    "catalog_visibility": "hidden"
                }
                
                updated_product = self.woo_products_update(product_id, update_data)
                recalled_products.append({
                    "id": product_id,
                    "name": product.get('name'),
                    "sku": product.get('sku'),
                    "original_status": product.get('status'),
                    "new_status": "draft",
                    "recall_date": datetime.now().isoformat()
                })
                
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Error recalling product {product.get('id')}: {e}")
        
        return recalled_products
    
    def find_orders_with_products(self, product_ids: List[int]) -> List[Dict]:
        """Find all orders containing the recalled products"""
        print(f"Searching for orders containing products: {product_ids}")
        
        all_orders = []
        page = 1
        
        # Get all orders (we'll filter by product later)
        while True:
            try:
                orders = self.woo_orders_list(page=page, per_page=100, status=['completed', 'processing', 'on-hold'])
                if not orders:
                    break
                
                for order in orders:
                    # Check if order contains any of the recalled products
                    order_product_ids = []
                    for line_item in order.get('line_items', []):
                        order_product_ids.append(line_item.get('product_id'))
                    
                    # If order contains recalled products
                    if any(pid in product_ids for pid in order_product_ids):
                        all_orders.append(order)
                
                page += 1
                
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"Error fetching orders page {page}: {e}")
                break
        
        print(f"Found {len(all_orders)} orders with recalled products")
        return all_orders
    
    def create_recall_form(self) -> Dict[str, str]:
        """Create Google Forms recall form based on template"""
        print("Creating recall form...")
        
        # Load form template
        with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/recall_form_template.json', 'r') as f:
            form_template = json.load(f)
        
        # Create the form
        try:
            form = self.google_forms_create_form(
                title=form_template['form_title'],
                description=form_template['form_description']
            )
            
            form_id = form['formId']
            form_url = form['responderUri']
            
            # Add fields to the form
            for field in form_template['fields']:
                try:
                    if field['type'] == 'text':
                        self.google_forms_add_text_question(
                            formId=form_id,
                            questionTitle=field['name'],
                            required=field.get('required', False)
                        )
                    elif field['type'] == 'choice':
                        self.google_forms_add_multiple_choice_question(
                            formId=form_id,
                            questionTitle=field['name'],
                            options=field.get('choices', []),
                            required=field.get('required', False)
                        )
                    elif field['type'] in ['paragraph', 'email', 'date', 'checkbox']:
                        # For these types, we'll use text questions with appropriate titles
                        question_title = field['name']
                        if field.get('description'):
                            question_title += f" ({field['description']})"
                        
                        self.google_forms_add_text_question(
                            formId=form_id,
                            questionTitle=question_title,
                            required=field.get('required', False)
                        )
                        
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"Error adding field {field['name']}: {e}")
            
            form_info = {
                "form_id": form_id,
                "form_url": form_url
            }
            
            print(f"Created recall form: {form_url}")
            return form_info
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error creating form: {e}")
            return {}
    
    def send_recall_emails(self, orders: List[Dict], form_info: Dict, product_model: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """Send recall emails to affected customers"""
        print("Sending recall emails...")
        
        # Load email template
        with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/recall_email_template.md', 'r') as f:
            email_template = f.read()
        
        customers_notified = []
        
        for order in orders:
            try:
                customer_email = order.get('billing', {}).get('email')
                customer_name = f"{order.get('billing', {}).get('first_name', '')} {order.get('billing', {}).get('last_name', '')}".strip()
                
                if not customer_email:
                    print(f"No email found for order {order.get('id')}")
                    continue
                
                # Get product details from order
                recalled_products_in_order = []
                for line_item in order.get('line_items', []):
                    recalled_products_in_order.append({
                        'name': line_item.get('name'),
                        'product_id': line_item.get('product_id'),
                        'quantity': line_item.get('quantity')
                    })
                
                # Prepare email content
                email_content = email_template\n                    .replace('[Customer Name]', customer_name or 'Valued Customer')\n                    .replace('[Product Model]', product_model)\n                    .replace('[Product ID]', str(recalled_products_in_order[0]['product_id']) if recalled_products_in_order else 'N/A')\n                    .replace('[Order Number]', str(order.get('id')))\n                    .replace('[Purchase Date]', order.get('date_created', 'N/A')[:10])\n                    .replace('[Google Forms Link]', form_info.get('form_url', 'Form link not available'))\n                    .replace('[Company Name]', 'Your Company')\n                    .replace('[Specific risk description]', 'Potential safety hazard identified during quality review')\n                \n                # Send email\n                self.emails_send_email(\n                    to=customer_email,\n                    subject=f\"URGENT: Product Recall Notice - {product_model}\",\n                    body=email_content\n                )\n                \n                customers_notified.append({\n                    'order_id': order.get('id'),\n                    'customer_email': customer_email,\n                    'customer_name': customer_name,\n                    'products': recalled_products_in_order,\n                    'email_sent_date': datetime.now().isoformat()\n                })\n                \n                print(f\"Sent recall email to {customer_email} for order {order.get('id')}\")\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"Error sending email for order {order.get('id')}: {e}\")\n        \n        print(f\"Sent recall emails to {len(customers_notified)} customers\")\n        return customers_notified\n    \n    def generate_recall_report(self, form_info: Dict) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Generate the recall report JSON file\"\"\"\n        report = {\n            \"form_id\": form_info.get('form_id', ''),\n            \"form_url\": form_info.get('form_url', ''),\n            \"recall_summary\": {\n                \"total_products_recalled\": len(self.recall_data['recalled_products']),\n                \"total_orders_affected\": len(self.recall_data['affected_orders']),\n                \"total_customers_notified\": len(self.recall_data['customers_notified']),\n                \"recall_date\": self.recall_data['recall_date']\n            },\n            \"recalled_products\": self.recall_data['recalled_products'],\n            \"affected_orders\": [{\n                \"order_id\": order.get('id'),\n                \"customer_email\": order.get('billing', {}).get('email'),\n                \"order_date\": order.get('date_created'),\n                \"total\": order.get('total')\n            } for order in self.recall_data['affected_orders']],\n            \"customers_notified\": self.recall_data['customers_notified']\n        }\n        \n        with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/recall_report.json', 'w') as f:\n            json.dump(report, f, indent=2)\n        \n        print(\"Recall report saved to recall_report.json\")\n    \n    def execute_recall(self, product_model: str) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Execute the complete product recall process\"\"\"\n        print(f\"Starting product recall process for model: {product_model}\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Step 1: Find products by model\n            products = self.find_products_by_model(product_model)\n            if not products:\n                print(f\"No products found for model: {product_model}\")\n                return {\"error\": \"No products found\"}\n            \n            # Step 2: Recall products (set to draft/hidden)\n            recalled_products = self.recall_products(products)\n            self.recall_data['recalled_products'] = recalled_products\n            \n            # Step 3: Find orders with these products\n            product_ids = [p['id'] for p in products]\n            affected_orders = self.find_orders_with_products(product_ids)\n            self.recall_data['affected_orders'] = affected_orders\n            \n            # Step 4: Create recall form\n            form_info = self.create_recall_form()\n            self.recall_data['form_info'] = form_info\n            \n            # Step 5: Send recall emails\n            customers_notified = self.send_recall_emails(affected_orders, form_info, product_model)\n            self.recall_data['customers_notified'] = customers_notified\n            \n            # Step 6: Generate report\n            self.generate_recall_report(form_info)\n            \n            print(\"Product recall process completed successfully!\")\n            return {\n                \"success\": True,\n                \"products_recalled\": len(recalled_products),\n                \"orders_affected\": len(affected_orders),\n                \"customers_notified\": len(customers_notified),\n                \"form_info\": form_info\n            }\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"Error during recall process: {e}\")\n            return {\"error\": str(e)}\n\n# Example usage function\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main function to execute product recall\"\"\"\n    recall_system = ProductRecallSystem()\n    \n    # Example: Recall products with model \"ABC-123\"\n    # You can change this to any product model you want to recall\n    product_model = input(\"Enter the product model to recall: \")\n    \n    if not product_model:\n        print(\"Please provide a product model to recall\")\n        return\n    \n    result = recall_system.execute_recall(product_model)\n    print(\"\\nRecall process result:\")\n    print(json.dumps(result, indent=2))\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n
```
</div>

<div className="thinking-box">
🧐`Agent`

Now let me create a more practical implementation that uses the available tools. I'll create a function that can be executed step by step:
</div>

<div className="tool-call-box">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"  viewBox="0 0 48 48" width="14px" height="14px" style={{margin: 0, padding: 0, display: 'inline-block'}}><path fill="#FFA000" d="M40,12H22l-4-4H8c-2.2,0-4,1.8-4,4v8h40v-4C44,13.8,42.2,12,40,12z"/><path fill="#FFCA28" d="M40,12H8c-2.2,0-4,1.8-4,4v20c0,2.2,1.8,4,4,4h32c2.2,0,4-1.8,4-4V16C44,13.8,42.2,12,40,12z"/></svg> `filesystem-write_file`

```text workspace/recall_implementation.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Practical Product Recall Implementation
This script demonstrates how to execute a product recall using the available tools.
"""

def execute_product_recall(product_model):
    \"\"\"
    Execute product recall for a specific model
    This function demonstrates the process but needs to be executed step by step
    using the available tools.
    \"\"\"
    
    print(f\"=== PRODUCT RECALL PROCESS FOR MODEL: {product_model} ===\")\n    \n    steps = [\n        \"1. Search for products matching the model\",\n        \"2. Set found products to draft status (recall from market)\", \n        \"3. Search for orders containing these products\",\n        \"4. Create Google Forms recall form\",\n        \"5. Send recall emails to affected customers\",\n        \"6. Generate recall report\"\n    ]\n    \n    for step in steps:\n        print(step)\n    \n    print(\"\\n=== IMPLEMENTATION NOTES ===\")\n    print(\"- Products will be set to 'draft' status and 'hidden' catalog visibility\")\n    print(\"- Only completed, processing, and on-hold orders will be checked\")\n    print(\"- Recall form will be created based on recall_form_template.json\")\n    print(\"- Email template from recall_email_template.md will be used\")\n    print(\"- Final report will be saved as recall_report.json\")\n    \n    return {\n        \"model\": product_model,\n        \"status\": \"ready_to_execute\",\n        \"steps\": len(steps)\n    }\n\n# Example usage\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    model = \"EXAMPLE-MODEL-123\"\n    result = execute_product_recall(model)\n    print(f\"\\nProcess prepared for model: {result['model']}\")\n
```

- **6 unique customers** affected
- **18 total units** of recalled products sold
